--------------------------------------------------
>> Issue: [B824:url_found] url_found
   Severity: Medium   Confidence: Medium
   Location: /home/blue/PyPIAgent/Dataset/study/unzip_benign/w3lib-2.3.1/w3lib-2.3.1/tests/test_url.py:386
   More Info: https://bandit.readthedocs.io/en/latest/plugins/b824_url_found.html
385	    # are not escaped.
386	    "https://@\\example.com",  # Invalid URL
387	    "https://\x80.example",  # Invalid domain name (non-visible character)
388	    "https://%80.example",  # Invalid domain name (non-visible character)
389	    "http://192.168.0.256",  # Invalid IP address
390	    "http://192.168.0.0.0",  # Invalid IP address / domain name
391	    "http://[2a01:5cc0:1:2::4]",  # https://github.com/scrapy/w3lib/issues/193
392	    "https://example.com:",  # Removes the :
393	    # Does not convert \ to /
394	    "https://example.com\\a",
395	    "https://example.com\\a\\b",
396	    # Encodes \ and / after the first one in the path
397	    "https://example.com/a/b",
398	    "https://example.com/a\\b",
399	    # Some path characters that RFC 2396 and RFC 3986 require escaping (%)
400	    # are not escaped.
401	    f"https://example.com/{PATH_TO_ENCODE}",
402	    # ? is removed

446	class UrlTests(unittest.TestCase):
447	    def test_safe_url_string(self):
448	        # Motoko Kusanagi (Cyborg from Ghost in the Shell)
449	        motoko = "\u8349\u8599 \u7d20\u5b50"
450	        self.assertEqual(
451	            safe_url_string(motoko),  # note the %20 for space
452	            "%E8%8D%89%E8%96%99%20%E7%B4%A0%E5%AD%90",
453	        )
454	        self.assertEqual(
455	            safe_url_string(motoko), safe_url_string(safe_url_string(motoko))
456	        )
457	        self.assertEqual(safe_url_string("©"), "%C2%A9")  # copyright symbol
458	        # page-encoding does not affect URL path
459	        self.assertEqual(safe_url_string("©", "iso-8859-1"), "%C2%A9")
